- Second term: `4.8185*epsilon**3`
- Third term: `5.4167*(T - 330.6)*sin(epsilon)` = `5.4167*T*sin(epsilon) - 1790.5*sin(epsilon)`

So GT = `-8.952*T*epsilon + 3059.5*epsilon + 4.8185*epsilon**3 + 5.4167*T*sin(epsilon) - 1790.5*sin(epsilon)`

The GT has these basis function components:
1. `T*epsilon` (linear in both)
2. `epsilon` (linear)
3. `epsilon**3` (cubic)
4. `T*sin(epsilon)` 
5. `sin(epsilon)`

Now I'll check each candidate for the ability to reproduce these exact basis functions.

**Key requirement:** The candidate must be able to produce terms: `T*epsilon`, `epsilon`, `epsilon**3`, `T*sin(epsilon)`, and `sin(epsilon)`.

Let me go through each candidate:

### Candidate 1: `T*c0 + T*c1*epsilon + c2*exp(c3/(c4+epsilon)) + c5*exp(c6*sin(c7*epsilon+c8)) + c9`
Has `T*epsilon` and `T` terms, but uses `exp(...)` and `exp(sin(...))` instead of `epsilon**3`, `T*sin(epsilon)`, `sin(epsilon)`. Cannot match.
Candidate 1 verdict: [NO MATCH]

### Candidate 2: `T*c0*epsilon + T*c1 + c2*log(c3*epsilon+1) + c4*exp(c5*sin(c6*epsilon+c7)) + c8*epsilon + c9`
Has `T*epsilon`, `T`, `log(...)`, `exp(sin(...))`, `epsilon`. Missing `epsilon**3` and `T*sin(epsilon)`.
Candidate 2 verdict: [NO MATCH]

### Candidate 3: `T*c0*exp(c1*epsilon) + T*c2*exp(c3*epsilon) + c4*log(c5*epsilon+1) + c6*exp(c7*sin(c8*epsilon+c9))`
Uses `T*exp(...)` which can't produce both `T*epsilon` and `T*sin(epsilon)` exactly.
Candidate 3 verdict: [NO MATCH]

### Candidate 4: `T*c0 + T*c1*epsilon + c2 + c3*sin(c4*epsilon+c5) + c6*exp(c7*sin(c8*epsilon+c9))`
Has `T`, `T*epsilon`, constant, `sin(...)`. Missing `epsilon**3` and `T*sin(epsilon)`.
Candidate 4 verdict: [NO MATCH]

### Candidate 5: `T*c0 + T*c1*epsilon + T*c2*epsilon**2 + c3*epsilon + c4*sin(c5*log(c6*|epsilon|+1)+c7) + c8*exp(c9*epsilon)`
Has `T*epsilon**2` but GT needs `epsilon**3`. Missing `T*sin(epsilon)`. Has `exp(epsilon)` which is wrong basis.
Candidate 5 verdict: [NO MATCH]

### Candidate 6: `T*c0 + T*c1*epsilon + c2*exp(c3*epsilon) + c4*epsilon/(c5+epsilon) + c6*exp(c7*sin(c8*epsilon+c9))`
Missing `epsilon**3`, `T*sin(epsilon)`, `sin(epsilon)`.
Candidate 6 verdict: [NO MATCH]

### Candidate 7: `T*c0 + T*c1*epsilon + c2*epsilon + c3*exp(c4*sin(c5*epsilon+c6))`
Missing `epsilon**3`, `T*sin(epsilon)`, `sin(epsilon)`.

### Candidate 8: `T*c0 + T*c1*epsilon + c2 + c3*epsilon + c4*exp(c5*sin(c6*epsilon+c7))`
Missing `epsilon**3`, `T*sin(epsilon)`, `sin(epsilon)`.

### Candidate 9: `T*c0 + T*c1*epsilon + T*c2*sin(c3*epsilon+c4) + c5*epsilon + c6*exp(c7*sin(c8*epsilon+c9))`
Has `T*sin(c3*epsilon+c4)` which with c3=1, c4=0 gives `T*sin(epsilon)`. Has `T*epsilon`, `T`, `epsilon`. But needs `epsilon**3` and `sin(epsilon)`. The `exp(c7*sin(...))` cannot produce both `epsilon**3` and `sin(epsilon)`.
Candidate 9 verdict: [NO MATCH]

All T-dependent terms are multiplied by T. Has `T*sin(epsilon)` ✓, `T*epsilon` ✓, `T` ✓, `epsilon` ✓. But needs `epsilon**3` and `sin(epsilon)` (without T). The `T*log(...)` and `T*epsilon*log(...)` terms can't produce `epsilon**3` or `sin(epsilon)`.
